BalancerAccumulator

Git Source

Inherits: AccumulatorDelegable, SafeModule

Author: StakeDAO

This contract is used to claim all the rewards the locker has received from the different reward pools before sending them to Stake DAO's Liquidity Gauge (v4)

This contract is the authorized distributor of the BAL and USDC rewards in the gauge

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

State Variables

FEE_DISTRIBUTOR

Fee distributor address.

address public constant FEE_DISTRIBUTOR = BalancerProtocol.FEE_DISTRIBUTOR;

Functions

constructor

--- CONSTRUCTOR

Constructor

*If locker and gateway are the same, internal calls will be done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts. Here are some hardcoded parameters automatically set by the contract:

  • USDC is the reward token
  • BAL is the token
  • VeBAL is the veToken*

Note: throws: InvalidGateway if the provided gateway is a zero address

constructor(address _gauge, address _locker, address _governance, address _gateway)
    AccumulatorDelegable(
        _gauge,
        Common.USDC,
        _locker,
        _governance,
        BalancerProtocol.BAL,
        BalancerProtocol.VEBAL,
        BalancerProtocol.VE_BOOST,
        BalancerLocker.VE_BOOST_DELEGATION,
        0
    )
    SafeModule(_gateway);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_gaugeaddressAddress of the sdBAL-gauge contract
_lockeraddressAddress of the sdBAL locker
_governanceaddressAddress of the governance
_gatewayaddressAddress of the gateway

claimAndNotifyAll

--- OVERRIDDEN FUNCTIONS

Make the locker claim all the reward tokens before depositing them to the Liquidity Gauge (v4)

function claimAndNotifyAll() external override;

_notifyReward

function _notifyReward(address _tokenReward, uint256 _amount) internal override;

_execute_claimRewards

--- SAFE MODULE RELATED FUNCTIONS

function _execute_claimRewards() internal returns (uint256 claimed);

_execute_transfer

function _execute_transfer(uint256 amount) internal;

_getLocker

--- GETTERS

function _getLocker() internal view override returns (address);

version

function version() external pure virtual override returns (string memory);

name

function name() external view virtual override returns (string memory);

CurveAccumulator

Git Source

Inherits: AccumulatorDelegable, SafeModule

Authors: CurveAccumulator, StakeDAO

This contract is used to claim all the rewards the locker has received from the different reward pools before sending them to Stake DAO's Liquidity Gauge (v4)

This contract is the authorized distributor of the CRVUSD and CRV rewards in the gauge

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

Functions

constructor

--- CONSTRUCTOR

Constructor

*If locker and gateway are the same, internal calls will be done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts. Here are some hardcoded parameters automatically set by the contract:

  • CRVUSD is the reward token
  • CRV is the token
  • VeCRV is the veToken*

Note: throws: InvalidGateway if the provided gateway is a zero address

constructor(address _gauge, address _locker, address _governance, address _gateway)
    AccumulatorDelegable(
        _gauge,
        CurveProtocol.CRV_USD,
        _locker,
        _governance,
        CurveProtocol.CRV,
        CurveProtocol.VECRV,
        CurveProtocol.VE_BOOST,
        CurveLocker.VE_BOOST_DELEGATION,
        0
    )
    SafeModule(_gateway);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_gaugeaddressAddress of the sdCRV-gauge contract
_lockeraddressAddress of the sdCRV locker
_governanceaddressAddress of the governance
_gatewayaddressAddress of the gateway

CurveExchangeDepositor

Git Source

Inherits: DepositorBase

Author: StakeDAO

Contract that accepts tokens and locks them in the Locker, minting sdToken in return

Adapted for veCRV like Locker.

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

State Variables

pool

Address of the sdToken pool.

address public pool;

Functions

constructor

constructor(address _token, address _locker, address _minter, address _gauge, uint256 _maxLockDuration, address _pool)
    DepositorBase(_token, _locker, _minter, _gauge, _maxLockDuration);

deposit

Deposit using the sdToken pool.

function deposit(uint256 _amount, uint256 _minAmount, bool _stake, address _user) public;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_amountuint256Amount of tokens to deposit.
_minAmountuint256Minimum amount of tokens to receive.
_stakeboolWhether to stake the sdToken in the gauge.
_useraddressAddress of the user.

_swap

Swap tokens using the sdToken pool.

function _swap(uint256 _amount, uint256 _minAmount, address _receiver) internal returns (uint256);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_amountuint256Amount of tokens to swap.
_minAmountuint256Minimum amount of tokens to receive.
_receiveraddressAddress of the receiver.

setPool

Set the pool address.

function setPool(address _pool) external onlyGovernance;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_pooladdressAddress of the sdToken pool

Events

Deposited

Event emitted when tokens are deposited.

event Deposited(address indexed caller, address indexed user, uint256 amount, bool stake);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
calleraddressAddress of the caller.
useraddressAddress of the user.
amountuint256Amount of tokens deposited.
stakeboolWhether the sdToken is staked in the gauge.

Errors

MIN_AMOUNT_NOT_MET

Throwed when no enought minimum amount is met.

error MIN_AMOUNT_NOT_MET();

VoteType

enum VoteType {
    Ownership,
    Parameter
}

Vote

Git Source

struct Vote {
    uint256 _voteId;
    uint256 _yeaPct;
    uint256 _nayPct;
    VoteType _voteType;
}

CurveVoter

Git Source

Inherits: VoterBase

Author: StakeDAO

This contract manages all the voting related to Curve protocols

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

State Variables

VOTER_OWNERSHIP

--- CONSTANTS

Curve voter for ownership proposals

address public immutable VOTER_OWNERSHIP = CurveProtocol.VOTING_APP_OWNERSHIP;

VOTER_PARAMETER

Curve voter for parameter proposals

address public immutable VOTER_PARAMETER = CurveProtocol.VOTING_APP_PARAMETER;

CONTROLLER

Curve gauge controller

address public immutable CONTROLLER = CurveProtocol.GAUGE_CONTROLLER;

LOCKER

Curve locker

address public immutable LOCKER = CurveLocker.LOCKER;

Functions

constructor

constructor(address _gateway) VoterBase(_gateway);

votes

--- PUBLIC FUNCTIONS

Bundle ownership and parameter votes

The given vote type must be either Ownership (0) or Parameter (1)

Notes:

  • throws: WRONG_VOTE_TYPE when the vote type is not valid

  • throws: NotAuthorized when the caller is not allowed

function votes(Vote[] calldata _votes) external hasProposalsOrAllPermission;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_votesVote[]Array of votes to bundle

voteOwnership

Vote for a ownership proposal

Note: throws: NotAuthorized when the caller is not allowed

function voteOwnership(uint256 _voteId, uint256 _yeaPct, uint256 _nayPct) public hasProposalsOrAllPermission;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_voteIduint256The ID of the proposal
_yeaPctuint256Percent of votes in favor of the proposal
_nayPctuint256Percent of votes against the proposal

voteParameter

Vote for a parameter proposal

Note: throws: NotAuthorized when the caller is not allowed

function voteParameter(uint256 _voteId, uint256 _yeaPct, uint256 _nayPct) public hasProposalsOrAllPermission;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_voteIduint256The ID of the proposal
_yeaPctuint256Percent of votes in favor of the proposal
_nayPctuint256Percent of votes against the proposal

_votePercent

--- INTERNAL FUNCTIONS

Vote for a proposal

Note: throws: WRONG_PCT when the pct is not valid

function _votePercent(uint256 _voteId, uint256 _yeaPct, uint256 _nayPct, address _voter) internal;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_voteIduint256The ID of the proposal
_yeaPctuint256Percent of votes in favor of the proposal
_nayPctuint256Percent of votes against the proposal
_voteraddressThe address of the voter

_getLocker

Get the locker address

Must be implemented for the SafeModule contract

function _getLocker() internal view override returns (address);

_getController

function _getController() internal view override returns (address);

Errors

WRONG_PCT

--- EVENTS & ERRORS

Error emitted when the pct is different than the voter pct

error WRONG_PCT();

WRONG_VOTE_TYPE

Error emitted when the vote type is not valid (neither Ownership nor Parameter)

error WRONG_VOTE_TYPE();

VeCRVLocker

Git Source

Author: Stake DAO

Locker contract for locking tokens for a period of time compatible with the Voting Escrow contract from Curve

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

State Variables

depositor

Address of the depositor which will mint sdTokens.

address public depositor;

accumulator

Address of the accumulator which will accumulate rewards.

address public accumulator;

governance

Address of the governance contract.

address public governance;

futureGovernance

Address of the future governance contract.

address public futureGovernance;

token

Address of the token being locked.

address public immutable token;

veToken

Address of the Voting Escrow contract.

address public immutable veToken;

Functions

onlyGovernance

--- MODIFIERS

modifier onlyGovernance();

onlyGovernanceOrDepositor

modifier onlyGovernanceOrDepositor();

onlyGovernanceOrAccumulator

modifier onlyGovernanceOrAccumulator();

constructor

constructor(address _governance, address _token, address _veToken);

name

Returns the name of the locker.

function name() public pure virtual returns (string memory);

createLock

--- LOCKER MANAGEMENT

Create a lock for the contract on the Voting Escrow contract.

function createLock(uint256 _value, uint256 _unlockTime) external virtual onlyGovernanceOrDepositor;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_valueuint256Amount of tokens to lock
_unlockTimeuint256Duration of the lock

Increase the lock amount or duration for the contract on the Voting Escrow contract.

function increaseLock(uint256 _value, uint256 _unlockTime) external virtual onlyGovernanceOrDepositor;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_valueuint256Amount of tokens to lock
_unlockTimeuint256Duration of the lock

    external
    virtual
    onlyGovernanceOrAccumulator;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_feeDistributoraddressAddress of the fee distributor.
_tokenaddressAddress of the token to claim.
_recipientaddressAddress to send the tokens to.

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_recipientaddressAddress to send the tokens to

Functions

constructor

--- CONSTRUCTOR

Constructor

*If locker and gateway are the same, internal calls will be done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts. Here are some hardcoded parameters automatically set by the contract:

  • FXS is the reward token*

Notes:

  • throws: InvalidGateway if the provided gateway is a zero address

  • throws: FXTLDelegationFailed if the delegation fails

constructor(
    address _gauge,
    address _locker,
    address _governance,
    address _delegationRegistry,
    address _initialDelegate,
    address _gateway
)
    AccumulatorBase(_gauge, FraxProtocol.FXS, _locker, _governance)
    FXTLDelegation(_delegationRegistry, _initialDelegate)
    SafeModule(_gateway);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_gaugeaddressfraxtal gauge
_lockeraddressfraxtal locker
_governanceaddressgovernance
_delegationRegistryaddressdelegation registry
_initialDelegateaddressinitial delegate

FraxDepositor

Git Source

Inherits: DepositorBase, FXTLDelegation, SafeModule

Constructor

*If locker and gateway are the same, internal calls will be done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts. Here are some hardcoded parameters automatically set by the contract:

PendleAccumulator

Git Source

Inherits: AccumulatorDripping, SafeModule

Author: StakeDAO

This contract is used to claim all the rewards the locker has received from the different reward pools before sending them to Stake DAO's Liquidity Gauge (v4)

This contract is the authorized distributor of the WETH and PENDLE rewards in the gauge

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

constructor

--- CONSTRUCTOR

Initializes the Accumulator

*If locker and gateway are the same, internal calls will be done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts. Here are some hardcoded parameters automatically set by the contract:

  • WETH is the reward token
  • PENDLE is the token
  • VePENDLE is the veToken*

Note: throws: InvalidGateway if the provided gateway is a zero address

BalancerFeeDistributor

Git Source

Functions

claimToken

Claims all pending distributions of the provided token for a user.

It's not necessary to explicitly checkpoint before calling this function, it will ensure the FeeDistributor is up to date before calculating the amount of tokens to be claimed.

function claimToken(address user, address token) external returns (uint256);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
useraddress- The user on behalf of which to claim.
tokenaddress- The ERC20 token address to be claimed.

Returns

NameTypeDescription
<none>uint256The amount of token sent to user as a result of claiming.

claimTokens

Claims a number of tokens on behalf of a user.

A version of claimToken which supports claiming multiple tokens on behalf of user. See claimToken for more details.

function claimTokens(address user, address[] calldata tokens) external returns (uint256[] memory);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
useraddress- The user on behalf of which to claim.
tokensaddress[]- An array of ERC20 token addresses to be claimed.

Returns

NameTypeDescription
<none>uint256[]An array of the amounts of each token in tokens sent to user as a result of claiming.

ILockerToken

Git Source

Inherits: IZeroLocker

Author: Curve Finance

Votes have a weight depending on time, so that users are committed to the future of (whatever they are voting for)

*Vote weight decays linearly over time. Lock time cannot be more than MAXTIME (4 years).

Voting escrow to have time-weighted votes

Votes have a weight depending on time, so that users are committed

to the future of (whatever they are voting for).

The weight in this implementation is linear, and lock cannot be more than maxtime:

w ^

1 + /

| /

| /

| /

|/c

0 +--------+------> time

maxtime (4 years?)*

IPendleFeeDistributor

Git Source

Functions

claimRetail

Submit total fee and proof to claim outstanding amount. Fee will be sent as raw ETH, so receiver should be an EOA or have receive() function.

function claimRetail(address receiver, uint256 totalAccrued, bytes32[] calldata proof)
    external
    returns (uint256 amountOut);

claimProtocol

Claim all outstanding fees for the specified pools. This function is intended for use by protocols that have contacted the Pendle team. Note that the fee will be sent in raw ETH, so the receiver should be an EOA or have a receive() function.

Protocols should not use claimRetail, as it can make getProtocolFeeData unreliable.

function claimProtocol(address receiver, address[] calldata pools)
    external
    returns (uint256 totalAmountOut, uint256[] memory amountsOut);

enableModule

function enableModule(address module) external;

NameTypeDescription
moduleaddressModule to be whitelisted.

execTransactionFromModule

Execute operation (0: Call, 1: DelegateCall) to to with value (Native Token)

Function is virtual to allow overriding for L2 singleton to emit an event for indexing.

function execTransactionFromModule(address to, uint256 value, bytes memory data, Enum.Operation operation)
    external
    returns (bool success);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
toaddressDestination address of module transaction.

function execTransactionFromModuleReturnData(address to, uint256 value, bytes memory data, Enum.Operation operation)
    external

NameTypeDescription

Returns

execTransaction

Executes a operation {0: Call, 1: DelegateCall}} transaction to to with value (Native Currency) and pays gasPrice * gasLimit in gasToken token to refundReceiver.

*The fees are always transferred, even if the user transaction fails. This method doesn't perform any sanity check of the transaction, such as:

  • if the contract at to address has code or not
  • if the gasToken is a contract or not It is the responsibility of the caller to perform such checks.*
function execTransaction(
    address to,
    uint256 value,
    bytes calldata data,
    Enum.Operation operation,
    uint256 safeTxGas,
    uint256 baseGas,
    uint256 gasPrice,
    address gasToken,
    address payable refundReceiver,
    bytes memory signatures
) external returns (bool success);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
toaddressDestination address of Safe transaction.
valueuint256Ether value of Safe transaction.
databytesData payload of Safe transaction.
operationEnum.OperationOperation type of Safe transaction.
safeTxGasuint256Gas that should be used for the Safe transaction.
baseGasuint256Gas costs that are independent of the transaction execution(e.g. base transaction fee, signature check, payment of the refund)
gasPriceuint256Gas price that should be used for the payment calculation.
gasTokenaddressToken address (or 0 if ETH) that is used for the payment.
refundReceiveraddress payableAddress of receiver of gas payment (or 0 if tx.origin).
signaturesbytesSignature data that should be verified. Can be packed ECDSA signature ({bytes32 r}{bytes32 s}{uint8 v}), contract signature (EIP-1271) or approved hash.

Returns

NameTypeDescription
successboolBoolean indicating transaction's success.

getOwners

Returns a list of Safe owners.

function getOwners() external view returns (address[] memory);

Returns

NameTypeDescription
<none>address[]Array of Safe owners.

addOwnerWithThreshold

function addOwnerWithThreshold(address owner, uint256 _threshold) external;

poke

Called by users to update voting balances in voting rewards contracts.

Parameters

NameTypeDescription

_tokenIduint256Id of veNFT whose balance you wish to update.

vote

Called by users to vote for pools. Votes distributed proportionally based on weights. Can only vote or deposit into a managed NFT once per epoch. Can only vote for gauges that have not been killed.

Weights are distributed proportional to the sum of the weights in the array. Throws if length of _poolVote and _weights do not match.

function vote(address _ve, uint256 _tokenId, uint160[] calldata _poolVote, uint256[] calldata _weights) external;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_veaddressAddress of ve token.
_tokenIduint256Id of veNFT you are voting with.
_poolVoteuint160[]Array of pool ids you are voting for.
_weightsuint256[]Weights of pools.

reset

Called by users to reset voting state. Required if you wish to make changes to veNFT state (e.g. merge, split, deposit into managed etc). Cannot reset in the same epoch that you voted in. Can vote or deposit into a managed NFT again after reset.

function reset(address _ve, uint256 _tokenId) external;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_veaddressAddress of ve token.
_tokenIduint256Id of veNFT you are reseting.

forceReset

Force reset a veNFT.

Throws if not called by VOTER_GOVERNOR_ROLE

function forceReset(address _ve, uint256 _tokenId) external;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_veaddressAddress of ve token.
_tokenIduint256Id of veNFT you are reseting.

depositManaged

Called by users to deposit into a managed NFT. Can only vote or deposit into a managed NFT once per epoch. Note that NFTs deposited into a managed NFT will be re-locked to the maximum lock time on withdrawal.

Throws if not approved or owner. Throws if managed NFT is inactive. Throws if depositing within privileged window (one hour prior to epoch flip).

function depositManaged(address _ve, uint256 _tokenId, uint256 _mTokenId) external;

withdrawManaged

Called by users to withdraw from a managed NFT. Cannot do it in the same epoch that you deposited into a managed NFT. Can vote or deposit into a managed NFT again after withdrawing. Note that the NFT withdrawn is re-locked to the maximum lock time.

function withdrawManaged(address _ve, uint256 _tokenId) external;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_veaddressAddress of ve token.
_tokenIduint256Id of veNFT you are withdrawing from.

Structs

LockedBalance

Structure to store locked balance information

struct LockedBalance {
    uint256 amount;
    uint256 end;
    uint256 start;
    uint256 power;
}

Properties

NameTypeDescription
amountuint256Amount of tokens locked
enduint256End time of the lock period (timestamp)
startuint256Start time of the lock period (timestamp)
poweruint256Additional parameter, potentially for governance or staking power

Call the execute function in another compatible contract

    external
    onlyGovernanceOrAllowed
    returns (bool success_, bytes memory result_);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription

_toaddressAddress of the contract to interact with the execute()
_valueuint256Value to send to the _to contract.
_databytesData to send to the _to contract.

Returns

NameTypeDescription

SafeModule

Git Source

Author: StakeDAO

Defining logic to call execute as a Safe module on the locker

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

State Variables

GATEWAY

--- CONSTANT

The gateway contract address

address public immutable GATEWAY;

Functions

constructor

Constructor for the SafeModule contract

The address of the gateway can be the same as the locker. In that case, the execution is done directly on the target from the gateway. Otherwise, the gateway will pass the execution to the locker to call the target contracts.

Note: throws: InvalidGateway if the provided gateway is a zero address

constructor(address _gateway);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_gatewayaddressThe address of the gateway contract.

_executeTransaction

--- INTERNAL FUNCTIONS

Executes a transaction through the Safe module system

Handle execution through either the gateway directly or through a locker's execute function

Note: throws: ExecFromSafeModuleFailed if the Safe module execution fails

function _executeTransaction(address _target, bytes memory _data) internal returns (bytes memory returnData);

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_targetaddressThe contract address to execute the transaction on
_databytesThe calldata to execute on the target contract

Returns

NameTypeDescription
returnDatabytesThe data returned from the executed transaction

version

Get the version of the contract Version follows the Semantic Versioning (https://semver.org/) Major version is increased when backward compatibility is broken in this base contract. Minor version is increased when new features are added in this base contract. Patch version is increased when child contracts are updated.

function version() external pure virtual returns (string memory);

AccumulatorDelegable

Git Source

Inherits: AccumulatorBase

This contract is an extension of the AccumulatorBase, designed to manage and distribute rewards to a delegation contract in a decentralized finance (DeFi) protocol. It leverages the veBoost mechanism to enhance reward distribution without transferring governance rights. The contract holds reward tokens and distributes them to a specified delegation contract based on the boost received and the balance of veTokens (e.g., veCRV). It applies a multiplier to the calculated delegation share, allowing for flexible reward strategies.

AccumulatorDripping

Git Source

Inherits: AccumulatorBase

Author: StakeDAO

Abstract contract for distributing ERC20 rewards over a fixed number of weekly steps, each step making an equal share of the available balance claimable. Designed for gas efficiency, modularity, and predictable reward flows.

  • Distributes rewards in equal weekly steps (aligned to EVM week boundaries).
  • Distribution state is packed for gas efficiency.
  • New distribution can only start when the previous is over and balance is nonzero.
  • At each step, claimable reward = current balance / remaining steps.
  • Missed steps are not compounded; distribution resumes at the next eligible call.
  • Additional tokens sent during an active distribution are included in future steps.
  • No overlapping distributions; last step drains remaining balance.
  • Inheriting contract must call advanceDistributionStep() after distributing. Example usage:
function claimReward() external {
uint256 reward = calculateDistributableReward();
require(reward > 0, "No reward available");
_sendReward(msg.sender, reward);
advanceDistributionStep();
}
```*

**Note:**
contact: contact@stakedao.org

### PERIOD_LENGTH
--- IMMUTABLES

A fixed-length interval defining by how many active weeks the reward is dripped equally.

startNewDistribution

Start a new distribution.

This function must be called once the distribution of the current distribution is done.

Notes:

  • throws: will throw if the distribution is still ongoing.

  • throws: will throw if there is no balance to distribute for the new distribution.

function startNewDistribution() internal;

advanceDistributionStep

Move to the next distribution step.

This function must be called once the distribution of the current step is done.

Note: throws: will throw if the distribution is already over because of the subtraction of the remaining periods.

function advanceDistributionStep() internal;

calculateDistributableReward

Calculate the reward available for claiming.

*1. The reward per step is calculated as the current contract balance divided by the number of remaining periods. This means:

  • If there is any rounding in previous steps, the last step will always distribute the remaining balance, ensuring the contract is fully drained by the end of the distribution.
  • If additional reward tokens are sent to this contract during an active distribution, those tokens will be included in the distribution for the remaining steps.
  1. The balance of rewardToken is used to calculate the current claimable reward. The rewardToken address is the one passed to the constructor of this contract and stored by the AccumulatorBase contract.
  2. This function do not automatically move to the next step of the distribution. If the reward are transferred, it is the responsibility of the caller to call advanceDistributionStep to move to the next step.*
function calculateDistributableReward() internal view returns (uint256 reward);

Returns

NameTypeDescription
rewarduint256The reward available for claiming.

state

The state of the contract.

*The contract uses a minimalistic state machine pattern to manage the lifecycle of locked tokens:

  1. At construction time, the contract is in the ACTIVE state.
  2. The contract can be shutdown by the governance at any time, transitioning the contract to the CANCELED state. This is a terminal state and cannot be reverted. Here's the State Machine Diagram: +--------------+ | ACTIVE | +--------------+ | shutdown | +--------------+ | CANCELED | +--------------+ Transitions:
  • ACTIVE -> CANCELED: via shutdown()*

deposit

Deposit tokens, and receive sdToken or sdTokenGauge in return.

If the lock is true, the tokens are directly sent to the locker and increase the lock amount as veToken. If the lock is false, the tokens are sent to this contract until someone locks them. A small percent of the deposit is used to incentivize users to lock the tokens. If the stake is true, the sdToken is staked in the gauge that distributes rewards. If the stake is false, the sdToken is sent to the user.

LockerPreLaunch

Git Source

Inherits: IPreLaunchLocker

A contract that enables secure token locking before full protocol deployment. The LockerPreLaunch serves as a solution for token locking during a protocol's pre-launch phase. Unlike traditional lockers that require the complete protocol stack to be deployed, this contract allows users to lock their tokens before the full protocol deployment. Key Features:

  • Token Deposit: Users can deposit tokens which are securely held in the contract
  • Pre-Launch Locking: Enables token locking mechanism before the full protocol deployment
  • Immediate sdToken Minting: Mints sdTokens to users immediately upon deposit with 1:1 ratio
  • Direct Gauge Integration: Optional direct staking of sdTokens into gauge upon deposit
  • Safety Net: Includes a refund mechanism if the project launch is canceled State Machine:
  • IDLE: Initial state where: Users can deposit tokens via deposit() with optional immediate gauge staking Governance can activate locker via lock(), transferring the initial tokens to depositor and moving state to ACTIVE Governance can cancel locker via cancelLocker() and modify the state to CANCELED Anyone can force cancel after delay via forceCancelLocker() and modify the state to CANCELED
  • ACTIVE: Activated state where: No more deposits, withdrawals or cancellations possible The user is now connected to the protocol via the depositor contract and the associated locker/gauge contracts
  • CANCELED: Terminal state where: Supports withdrawal of both staked and unstaked sdTokens No deposits or state changes possible

This contract implements a state machine with three states: IDLE, ACTIVE, and CANCELED

*The contract uses a state machine pattern to manage the lifecycle of locked tokens:

  1. Users deposit tokens in IDLE state, receiving sdTokens immediately
  2. Governance can either: a) Activate the locker (IDLE -> ACTIVE) connecting it to the protocol via depositor b) Cancel the launch (IDLE -> CANCELED) enabling refunds of the initial tokens
  3. Both ACTIVE and CANCELED are terminal states*

Note: contact: contact@stakedao.org

state

The state of the locker.

*The contract uses a state machine pattern to manage the lifecycle of locked tokens:

  1. Users deposit tokens in IDLE state
  2. Governance can either: a) Activate the locker (IDLE -> ACTIVE) connecting it to the protocol b) Cancel the launch (IDLE -> CANCELED) enabling refunds
  3. Both ACTIVE and CANCELED are terminal states Here's the State Machine Diagram: +-------------------+ | IDLE | +-------------------+ | | lock | | cancelLocker | | +---------+ +-----------+ | ACTIVE | | CANCELED | +---------+ +-----------+ Transitions:
  • IDLE -> ACTIVE: via lock()
  • IDLE -> CANCELED: via cancelLocker()
  • ACTIVE: terminal state
  • CANCELED: terminal state*

  • reverts: REQUIRED_PARAM if the given address is zero.

  • reverts: CANNOT_LOCK_ACTIVE_OR_CANCELED_LOCKER if the contract is not in the idle state when trying to lock.

  • reverts: INVALID_TOKEN if the given address is not a valid depositor.

  • reverts: INVALID_GAUGE if the given address is not a valid gauge.

  • reverts: INVALID_SD_TOKEN if the given address is not a valid sdToken.

  • reverts: NOTHING_TO_LOCK if there is nothing to lock.

  • reverts: TOKEN_NOT_TRANSFERRED_TO_LOCKER if the locker contract doesn't hold the initial tokens.

function lock(address _depositor) external onlyGovernance;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
_depositoraddressThe address of the depositor.

withdraw

--- EMERGENCY METHODS

Withdraw the previously deposited tokens if the launch has been canceled. This is an escape hatch for users.

This function can only be called if the locker is in the canceled state.

Notes:

  • reverts: REQUIRED_PARAM if the given amount is zero.

  • reverts: CANNOT_WITHDRAW_IDLE_OR_ACTIVE_LOCKER if the locker is not in the canceled state.

function withdraw(uint256 amount, bool staked) external;

Parameters

NameTypeDescription
amountuint256Amount of tokens to withdraw.
stakedboolIndicates if the sdTokens were staked in the gauge or not. If true, the function will handle the withdrawal of sdTokens staked in the gauge before burning them. The caller must have approved this contract to transfer the gauge token. If false, the function will simply burn the sdToken held by the caller.

cancelLocker

Set the state of the locker as CANCELED. It only happens if the launch of the campaign has been canceled.

Notes:

  • reverts: ONLY_GOVERNANCE if the caller is not the stored governance address.

  • reverts: CANNOT_CANCEL_ACTIVE_OR_CANCELED_LOCKER if the locker is active.

function cancelLocker() external onlyGovernance;

forceCancelLocker

Force cancel the locker. Can only be called if the locker is in the idle state and the timestamp is older than the force cancel delay. This function is an escape hatch allowing anyone to force cancel the locker if the governance is not responsive. When the locker is in the canceled state, the users can withdraw their previously deposited tokens.

Notes:

  • reverts: CANNOT_FORCE_CANCEL_ACTIVE_OR_CANCELED_LOCKER if the locker is not in the idle state.

  • reverts: CANNOT_FORCE_CANCEL_RECENTLY_CREATED_LOCKER if the locker is not old enough to be force canceled.

function forceCancelLocker() external;

transferGovernance

Note: reverts: ONLY_GOVERNANCE if the caller is not the stored governance address.

function transferGovernance(address _governance) external onlyGovernance;

Parameters

Error thrown when there is nothing to lock. This can happen if nobody deposited tokens before the locker was locked. In that case, the locker is useless.

Error thrown when the token is not transferred to the locker.

CANNOT_WITHDRAW_IDLE_OR_ACTIVE_LOCKER

CANNOT_FORCE_CANCEL_ACTIVE_OR_CANCELED_LOCKER

error CANNOT_FORCE_CANCEL_ACTIVE_OR_CANCELED_LOCKER();

Error thrown when the locker is not enough old to be force canceled.

error CANNOT_FORCE_CANCEL_RECENTLY_CREATED_LOCKER();

Redeem

Git Source

Inherits: Ownable2Step, ReentrancyGuard

--- IMPORTS

Allows users to redeem sdTokensincluding staked balancesfor the underlying token at a fixed conversion rate. Any pending gauge rewards are forwarded to the caller during redemption.

Ownership is transferred via the {Ownable2Step} pattern. The owner can sweep leftover token only after a 365day cooldown starting from the first successful redemption.

State Variables

token

--- IMMUTABLES

Token that users ultimately receive.

address public immutable token;

sdToken

sdToken that can be redeemed and burned.

Staking contract for sdToken balances.

address public immutable sdTokenGauge;

Conversion rate between sdToken and token expressed with 1e18 precision.

uint256 public immutable conversionRateWad;

reedeemCooldownDuration

The cooldown duration before the owner can retrieve unredeemed token.

uint256 public immutable reedeemCooldownDuration;

--- CONSTANTS --- STORAGE

Whether the redeem function has been called.

bool public isRedemptionFinalized;

Timestamp of the first redeem() call. Determines the cooldown window.

uint256 public firstRedeemTimestamp;

VoterPermissionManager

Git Source

Inherits: Governance

State Variables

BUFFER

--- CONSTANTS

Instead of using a traditional mapping that hashes the key to calculate the slot, we directly use the unique identifier of each module as the storage slot. The storage buffer exists to avoid future collisions. Note the owner of this contract takes one slot in storage (slot 0). The value of the buffer is equal to the keccak256 hash of the constant string ""STAKEDAO.LOCKER.V2.VOTER_ALLOWANCE_MANAGER.V1"", meaning the modules will be stored starting at slot 0x65a8012b7737dd00fb2623a75e13d3926cb7a6c59e6b502af4b6718938bb9be4. This is a gas cost optimization made possible due to the simplicity of the storage layout.

bytes32 internal constant BUFFER = keccak256("STAKEDAO.LOCKER.V2.VOTER_ALLOWANCE_MANAGER.V1");

Enums

Permission

--- STATE

Enum representing the different permission levels for voter actions.

  • NONE: Default permission. The address cannot call any permissioned functions.
  • PROPOSALS_ONLY: The address can call functions that interact with proposals, e.g., voting on protocol proposals.
  • GAUGES_ONLY: The address can call functions that interact with gauges, e.g., voting for gauge weights.
  • ALL: The address can call all permissioned functions, including both proposal-related and gauge-related actions.*
enum Permission {
    NONE,
    PROPOSALS_ONLY,
    GAUGES_ONLY,
    ALL
}
